              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>大草原上,狮子正<span class="label-words" data-wid="2007">紧</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2007">紧</span>地追赶一只羊。在追赶中,狮子超过了一只又一只站在旁边观望的羊,对那些靠得很近的羊,狮子却像没看见一样,一次次地放过。终于,那只被追赶的羊因跑不动而被狮子扑<span class="label-words" data-wid="1642">倒</span>了。为什么狮子不放弃原来那只,改去追赶离它更近的羊呢?原来狮子已经跑累了,而其他的羊并没有奔跑。如果在追赶的过程中改变<span class="label-words" data-wid="2179">目标</span>,那么,那些没有跑累的羊,会很快把狮子<span class="label-words" data-wid="2409">甩</span>在后面。</p>

              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>楚国有一个专门卖珠宝的商人,为了使自己的珠宝更畅销,他特地用名贵的木料做了许多小盒子,把珠宝<span class="label-words" data-wid="2834">装</span>在里面卖。这种<span class="label-words" data-wid="2834">装</span>珠宝的盒子<span class="label-words" data-wid="2801">制作</span>得非常漂亮,而且还散发出一种香味儿。有一个人看见<span class="label-words" data-wid="2834">装</span>珠宝的盒子既精致又美观,问明价钱后,就买了一个。那个人打开盒子,把里面的珠宝拿出来<span class="label-words" data-wid="2496">退</span>还给珠宝商,拿着空盒子走了。这就是<span class="label-words" data-wid="1550">成语</span>“买椟还珠”的由来。这个<span class="label-words" data-wid="1550">成语</span>比喻有些人只重视<span class="label-words" data-wid="2384">事物</span>的外表,却忽略了真正有<span class="label-words" data-wid="1945">价值</span>的东西,取舍不当。</p>

              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>有个教授做过这样一个调查:他曾仔细<span class="label-words" data-wid="1830">观察</span>过学生上课时选座位的情况,他发现有的学生总爱坐前排,有的则盲目随意,哪儿都坐,还有一些人<span class="label-words" data-wid="2422">似乎</span>特别钟情后面的座位。教授<span class="label-words" data-wid="1738">分别</span>记下了他们的名字。十年后,教授发现:爱坐前排的学生中,事业成功的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1460">比例</span>比其他两<span class="label-words" data-wid="2085">类</span>学生高很多。</p> 
               <p>其实,很多时候,并不是一定要站在最前面,或永远<span class="label-words" data-wid="1445">保持</span>第一的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2838">状态</span>，但是我们一定要有这种积极向上的心态。只有怀着一<span class="label-words" data-wid="2053">颗</span>积极向上的心,才能以最佳的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2838">状态</span>投入到学习和工作当中,才能取得理想的成绩。</p>
              </div>
             </div>

              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p><span class="label-words" data-wid="2177">某</span>电视台邀请一位成功的商人做<span class="label-words" data-wid="1943">嘉宾</span>,到场的观众<span class="label-words" data-wid="1743">纷纷</span>向他求教成功之道。但商人只是淡淡一笑,说:“还是出个题考考大家吧。<span class="label-words" data-wid="2177">某</span>个地方发现了金矿,很多人闻讯赶去,然而一条大河<span class="label-words" data-wid="1637">挡</span>住了他们的去路。换做是你,你会怎么做?”有人说<span class="label-words" data-wid="2296">绕</span>道走,也有人说游过去。商人含笑不语,最后说:“为什么<span class="label-words" data-wid="1733">非</span>得去淘金?为什么不买一条船开展营运呢?”商人继续说:“在那种情况下,你就是把船票价格要得再高,淘金的人也会心甘情愿购买,因为前面有金矿啊!”</p> 
               <p>想他人不曾想的,做他人不曾做的,这就是成功之道。困境在智者眼中往往意味着一个潜在的机遇。</p>
              </div>

              <div class="field-subject ans-hide">
               <p>有个小男孩儿在一家面包店买一个两块钱的面包,他觉得这个面包比平时买的要小，<span class="label-words" data-wid="1471">便</span>对<span class="label-words" data-wid="2079">老板</span>说:“你不觉得这个面包比平时的要小一些吗?”“哦,没关系,小一些你拿起来不就更轻便吗?”“我懂了。”小男孩儿说着,就把一块钱放在<span class="label-words" data-wid="1851">柜台</span>上,然后转身<span class="label-words" data-wid="1530">朝</span>店外走去。<span class="label-words" data-wid="2079">老板</span>叫住他:“喂，你付的面包钱不够!”小男孩儿说:“哦,没关系,少一些你数起来就会更容易。”</p>
              </div>

              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>过程是一<span class="label-words" data-wid="1793">根</span>线,结果是一个点。就拿登山来说,在登山的过程中,你可以走走停停,<span class="label-words" data-wid="2611">欣赏</span>鲜花,<span class="child-number">53</span>美景,<span class="label-words" data-wid="2582">享受</span>清风的抚摸,静听小鸟的鸣唱。这一路上的胜景,就好像用一根线串在一起,串成一连串的幸福,<span class="label-words" data-wid="2557">系</span>在心间。而登山的结果,就是登上山顶。也许在山项你能<span class="label-words" data-wid="2582">享受</span>到一种征服山峰的幸福，但这种幸福<span class="child-number">54</span>是暂时的，因为山顶只是一个点，你终究要从这个点走下来，随着你走下山顶，那种在山顶上的幸福感也就<span class="child-number">55</span>了。</p>

              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>为什么在飞机上打<span class="label-words" data-wid="2672">移动</span>电话很危险?原来,飞机在<span class="label-words" data-wid="2467">天空</span>中是按照规定的方向飞行的,<span class="child-number">57</span>飞行过程都要受到地面管理<span class="label-words" data-wid="2306">人员</span>的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2793">指挥</span>。飞机在飞行时需要<span class="child-number">58</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2177">某</span>种<span class="label-words" data-wid="2340">设备</span>与地面进行联系,这种<span class="label-words" data-wid="2340">设备</span>在接到地面<span class="label-words" data-wid="2793">指挥</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2806">中心</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1491">不断</span>发出的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2613">信号</span>后,<span class="child-number">59</span>。如果发现飞机离开了规定的方向,它就会<span class="child-number">60</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2850">自动</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1764">改正</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1611">错误</span>,保证飞机正常飞行。但是,当<span class="label-words" data-wid="2672">移动</span>电话工作时,它所发射的无线电波会影响飞机上的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2340">设备</span>和<span class="label-words" data-wid="2066">控制</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2560">系统</span>。因此,在飞机上是不能使用<span class="label-words" data-wid="2672">移动</span>电话的。</p>

               <p>植物也会“犯困”,<span class="label-words" data-wid="1461">比如</span>生长在水面的睡莲,每当旭日东<span class="label-words" data-wid="2353">升</span>时,它那美丽的花瓣就会慢慢舒<span class="label-words" data-wid="2749">展开</span>,<span class="label-words" data-wid="2422">似乎</span>正从甜蜜的睡梦中苏醒;而当夕阳西下时,它<span class="label-words" data-wid="1471">便</span>闭拢花瓣,重新进入睡眠<span class="label-words" data-wid="2838">状态</span>。由于它“昼醒晚睡”的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1848">规律</span>性特别<span class="label-words" data-wid="2166">明显</span>,故而获得了“睡莲”的芳名。</p>

            <div class="exercise-view exercise-dxz" data-eid="30905" data-lid="191" data-sid="96" data-pid="0" data-tid="14">
             <div class="exr-heading">
              <div class="exr-caption">
               Đề thi thật - Đề thi thật Bộ10 - Đọc hiểu đoạn văn

             <div class="field-heading">
              <div class="field-number">
               71-74
              </div> 
              <div class="field-image">
               <img src="http://f.hskcdn.com/res/exr/5/z/images/15/71-74.jpg" alt="">
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>一家濒临倒闭的食品公司为了起死回生，决定裁员。三种人被列入了栽员名单:一是清洁工,二是司机,三是仓管<span class="label-words" data-wid="2306">人员</span>。经理找他们谈话,说明了裁员的意图。清洁工说:“我们很重要,如果没有我们打扫卫生,哪有干净整洁的工作环境?大家怎么能全身心投入工作?”司机说:“我们很重要,这么多<span class="label-words" data-wid="1525">产品</span>,如果没有司机,怎么能<span class="label-words" data-wid="2647">迅速</span>销往市场?”仓管<span class="label-words" data-wid="2306">人员</span>说:“我们很重要,如果没有我们,这些食品岂不要被人偷光?”经理觉得他们说的话都很有<span class="label-words" data-wid="1648">道理</span>,权衡<span class="label-words" data-wid="2737">再三</span>决定不裁员。最后,经理在公司门口挂了一块儿大匾,上面写着:我很重要。</p> 
               <p>职工们每天上班时,第一眼看到的便是“我很重要”这4个字。不管是一线职工还是管理层,都认为<span class="label-words" data-wid="2118">领导</span>很重视他们,因此工作都很卖力。这几个字调动了全体职工的积极性,几年后公司<span class="label-words" data-wid="1471">便</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2647">迅速</span>崛起了。</p> 
               <p>任何时候都不要看轻自己,在关键<span class="label-words" data-wid="2367">时刻</span>,勇敢地说出“我很重要”,或许你的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2303">人生</span>会由此揭开全新的一页。</p>
              </div>

            <div class="exercise-view exercise-dxz" data-eid="30910" data-lid="191" data-sid="96" data-pid="0" data-tid="14">
             <div class="exr-heading">
              <div class="exr-caption">
               Đề thi thật - Đề thi thật Bộ10 - Đọc hiểu đoạn văn
              </div> 
              <div class="exr-progress">
               <span class="cur">75-78</span>/100
              </div>

             <div class="field-heading">
              <div class="field-number">
               75-78
              </div> 
              <div class="field-image">
               <img src="http://f.hskcdn.com/res/exr/5/z/images/15/75-78.jpg" alt="">
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>有个女孩儿用一个月的薪水,买了一件心仪已久的衣服。穿上新衣服的她,看着别人惊艳的眼神,心中<span class="label-words" data-wid="1565">充满</span>了<span class="label-words" data-wid="2856">自信</span>,工作也有了很大的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2013">进步</span>。</p> 
               <p>可是有一天,她发现衣服上的一枚纽扣儿不见了。那是一种<span class="label-words" data-wid="2626">形状</span>很奇特的纽扣儿,她<span class="label-words" data-wid="1716">翻</span>遍衣柜,也没有找到,于是就穿了另一件衣服去上班。到了公司,她觉得每个人看她的眼神都怪怪的,<span class="label-words" data-wid="2422">似乎</span>没有了那件衣服,自己仍然是个极平凡的女孩儿。她心里一直想着那件衣服,一整天都打不起精神,也没有了平日的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2856">自信</span>。</p> 
               <p>下班后,她在家里又找了一遍,<span class="label-words" data-wid="2671">依然</span>没有找到。随后她又跑遍了商店,也没有买到同样的纽扣儿,她的心情暗淡到了极点。<span class="label-words" data-wid="1598">从此</span>,那件衣服<span class="label-words" data-wid="1471">便</span>被束之高阁,女孩儿初穿它时的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2856">自信</span>与热情<span class="label-words" data-wid="2595">消失</span>得无影无踪,工作也慢慢消极起来。</p> 
               <p>天,一个朋友来访,<span class="label-words" data-wid="2199">偶然</span>看到了那件衣服,吃惊地问:“这么漂亮的衣服你怎么不穿呢?”她说:“丢了一枚扣子,又买不到同样的。”朋友笑着说:“那你可以把其他的扣子都换了啊,那不就一样了吗?”女孩儿听了非常高兴,于是选了她最喜欢的扣子,把原来的都换掉了。衣服美丽如初,她也重拾了灿烂的心情。</p> 
               <p>我们常常因为小小的缺憾而放弃一整件事,也常常因为放弃了一件事而使生活变得暗淡。如果我们能用一种全新的心情去替换失望,用笑容填满缺失,那么生命一样是<span class="label-words" data-wid="2504">完美</span>无憾的。</p>
              </div>
             </div>

            <div class="exercise-view exercise-dxz" data-eid="30915" data-lid="191" data-sid="96" data-pid="0" data-tid="14">
             <div class="exr-heading">
              <div class="exr-caption">
               Đề thi thật - Đề thi thật Bộ10 - Đọc hiểu đoạn văn
              </div> 
              <div class="exr-progress">
               <span class="cur">79-82</span>/100
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-heading">
              <div class="field-number">
               79-82
              </div> 
              <div class="field-image">
               <img src="http://f.hskcdn.com/res/exr/5/z/images/15/79-82.jpg" alt="">
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>王献之是著名书法家王羲之的儿子,自幼聪明好学。</p> 
               <p>一天,小献之问母亲:“我只要再写上三年,字就可以写得像父亲一样好了吧?”母亲<span class="label-words" data-wid="2655">摇</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2655">摇</span>头。“5年总行了吧?”母亲又<span class="label-words" data-wid="2655">摇</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2655">摇</span>头。小献之急了,“那您说要多长时间?”母亲说:“写完院里这18缸水,你的字才会有筋骨、有血肉。”</p> 
               <p>小献之有些不服,但什么也没说,一<span class="label-words" data-wid="2656">咬</span>牙又练了5年。一天,他把一大<span class="label-words" data-wid="1689">堆</span>写好的字拿给父亲看,希望听到几句表扬的话。谁知,王羲之边看边<span class="label-words" data-wid="2655">摇</span>头,当他看到一个“大”字时,才<span class="label-words" data-wid="2124">露</span>出了比较满意的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1478">表情</span>,并随手在“大”字下添了一个点儿,然后把字稿全部<span class="label-words" data-wid="2496">退</span>还给了献之。</p> 
               <p>献之仍然不服,又将全部的字抱给母亲看,并说:“您再仔细看看,我和父亲的字还有什么不同?”母亲指着王羲之在“大”加的那个点儿,叹了口气说:“吾儿磨尽三缸水,惟有一点似羲之。”</p> 
               <p>献之听后很泄气,说:“这样下去,什么时候才能赶上父亲呢?”母亲见他不再骄傲,<span class="label-words" data-wid="1471">便</span>鼓励道:“孩子,只要<span class="label-words" data-wid="1808">功夫</span>深,就没有过不去的河、<span class="label-words" data-wid="1716">翻</span>不过的山。你只要像这几年一样坚持不懈地练下去,就一定能<span class="label-words" data-wid="1612">达到</span>目的。”献之听后深有感触,又锲而不舍地练了下去。<span class="label-words" data-wid="1808">功夫</span>不负有心人,后来,献之的书法突飞猛进,字也<span class="label-words" data-wid="1612">达到</span>了和父亲一样力透纸背、炉火纯青的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1556">程度</span>。</p>
              </div>
             </div>

            <div class="exercise-view exercise-dxz" data-eid="30920" data-lid="191" data-sid="96" data-pid="0" data-tid="14">
             <div class="exr-heading">
              <div class="exr-caption">
               Đề thi thật - Đề thi thật Bộ10 - Đọc hiểu đoạn văn
              </div> 
              <div class="exr-progress">
               <span class="cur">83-86</span>/100
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-heading">
              <div class="field-number">
               83-86
              </div> 
              <div class="field-image">
               <img src="http://f.hskcdn.com/res/exr/5/z/images/15/83-86.jpg" alt="">
              </div> 
              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>地球上最热的地方在哪里?许多人认为是赤道<span class="label-words" data-wid="1661">地区</span>。其实，最热的地方并不在赤道。世界上有许多地方,像中国的塔克拉玛干<span class="label-words" data-wid="2323">沙漠</span>、非洲的撒哈拉大<span class="label-words" data-wid="2323">沙漠</span>等,白天的最高温度都超过了45℃;而赤道<span class="label-words" data-wid="1661">地区</span>,尽管阳光的照射很<span class="label-words" data-wid="2258">强烈</span>，但白天气温很少超过35℃。</p> 
               <p>这是因为赤道附近大多是海洋,海洋一方面能把太阳给它的热量传向深处;另一方面海水蒸发会消耗大量的热量,再加上海水的热容量大,水温的<span class="label-words" data-wid="2353">升</span>高速度要比<span class="label-words" data-wid="2125">陆地</span>慢。因此,白天赤道附近的温度不会急剧上<span class="label-words" data-wid="2353">升</span>。</p> 
               <p><span class="label-words" data-wid="2323">沙漠</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1661">地区</span>的情况就完全不同了。那里植物稀少、水<span class="label-words" data-wid="2846">资源</span>短缺,几乎没有可蒸发的水分,而且沙子热容量小、<span class="label-words" data-wid="2353">升</span>温快,热量不容易向地表下层<span class="label-words" data-wid="1584">传递</span>。因此,白天沙地<span class="label-words" data-wid="1476">表面</span>被太阳<span class="label-words" data-wid="2326">晒</span>得<span class="label-words" data-wid="1852">滚</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2442">烫</span>,而下层的沙子却是冷冰冰的。在<span class="label-words" data-wid="2323">沙漠</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1661">地区</span>,每当太阳<span class="label-words" data-wid="2124">露</span>面,气温就会急剧上<span class="label-words" data-wid="2353">升</span>,地表开始发<span class="label-words" data-wid="2442">烫</span>;到了中午,更是骄阳似火,有时最高气温可达55℃。</p> 
               <p>另外,赤道上的降雨要比<span class="label-words" data-wid="2323">沙漠</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="1661">地区</span>多,几乎每天下午都会下雨,这样一来,下午赤道<span class="label-words" data-wid="1661">地区</span>的温度<span class="label-words" data-wid="1471">便</span>不会<span class="label-words" data-wid="2353">升</span>得很高。而<span class="label-words" data-wid="2323">沙漠</span>里经常是大晴天,很少下雨，阳光从早晨一直照到<span class="label-words" data-wid="1438">傍晚</span>。所以,最热的地方不在赤道,而是在<span class="label-words" data-wid="2323">沙漠</span>里。</p>
              </div>
             </div> 
             <div class="field-body">
              <div class="field-children">

                <div class="field-heading">
                 <div class="field-number">

                 </div> 
                 <div class="field-question">
                  <p>根据上文，下列哪<span class="label-words" data-wid="2585">项</span>正确？</p>
                 </div>
                </div> 
                <div class="field-body">
                 <div class="field-items cols-lg-2">
                  <div class="field-option-wrap answer" data-no="0">
                   <div class="field-option">
                    <span class="field-no">A</span>

              <div class="field-subject">
               <p>唐太宗李世民堪称中国<span class="label-words" data-wid="1815">古代</span>少有的开明君主。他登上皇位后,吸取历史上的<span class="label-words" data-wid="1984">教训</span>,广开言路,鼓励大臣们多<span class="label-words" data-wid="2454">提</span>意见。魏征是一位敢于说话而且<span class="label-words" data-wid="2332">善于</span>言辞的大臣。唐太宗曾问魏征,<span class="label-words" data-wid="1900">皇帝</span><span class="label-words" data-wid="2316">如何</span>才能<span class="label-words" data-wid="1445">保持</span>头脑清醒而不昏庸?魏征的回答是:兼听则明,偏信则暗。意思是<span class="label-words" data-wid="1845">广泛</span>地听取大家的意见就能做到开明;偏信<span class="label-words" data-wid="2177">某</span>一个或<span class="label-words" data-wid="2177">某</span>些人就会变得昏庸。</p> 
               <p>有一年,宰相向唐太宗<span class="label-words" data-wid="1963">建议</span>:不满18岁的青年男子,只要身形高大、体格强壮,都可以应征入伍。唐太宗<span class="label-words" data-wid="2214">批准</span>了这个<span class="label-words" data-wid="1963">建议</span>,但奏章却多次被魏征驳回。唐太宗非常生气,于是召集众臣，当面训斥魏征。谁知魏征毫无惧色,并说道:“把湖水淘干,可以把鱼捕得一干二净,但第二年就没有鱼可捕了;把森林烧光,林中的野兽无处藏身,但第二年也就没有野兽可猎了。现在就把不满18岁的强壮男子都收入军队,不留任何余地,那么以后国家向谁去征<span class="label-words" data-wid="2411">税</span>呢?”几句话说得唐太宗恍然大悟,于是听从了魏征的意见,并重赏了他。</p>
              </div>

        var paperDate = new Date(), stopOffsetDate, timeLeft = 7200, timeTotal = 7200;
        paperDate.setSeconds(paperDate.getSeconds() + 7200);
        $('#paper-countdown').on('click', '.btn[data-op]', function () {
            var op = $(this).data('op');
            if(op === 'start' && stopOffsetDate){
                paperDate = new Date();
                paperDate.setHours(paperDate.getHours() + stopOffsetDate.hours);
                paperDate.setMinutes(paperDate.getMinutes() + stopOffsetDate.minutes);
                paperDate.setSeconds(paperDate.getSeconds() + stopOffsetDate.seconds);
                $('#paper-countdown').countdown('setFinalDate', paperDate);
            }
            $('#paper-countdown').countdown(op).find('.btn[data-op]').toggleClass('hide');
            $('#exercise-list').exerciseTest('resetTime');
        }).countdown(paperDate, function (event) {
            timeLeft = event.offset.hours * 60 * 60 + event.offset.minutes * 60 + event.offset.seconds;
            $('.cd-time', this).html(event.strftime('%H:%M:%S'));
        }).on('stoped.countdown', function (event) {
            stopOffsetDate = event.offset;
        });
        $('#exercise-list').on('slid.bs.carousel', function (e) {
            var $el = $(e.relatedTarget), index = $el.index();
            $('#exr-prev').prop('disabled', $el.prev().length === 0);
            if ($el.next().length > 0) {
                $('#exr-next').removeClass('hide');
                $('#exr-submit').addClass('hide');
            } else {
                $('#exr-next').addClass('hide');
                $('#exr-submit').removeClass('hide');
            }
            if (!$el.data('autoPlayed')) {
                $el.find('.circle-audio').autoPlay();
                $el.data('autoPlayed', 1);
            } else if (e.direction === 'left') {
                $el.prev().stopPlay();
            } else {
                $el.next().stopPlay();
            }
            $(this).exerciseTest('setSubmitParams', 'recent_index', index);
            activeAnswerSheetPanel(index);
        }).on('slide.bs.carousel', function (e) {
            $('.item.active .exercise-view', this).trigger('next.hsk.test');
        }).on('beforeSubmit', function (e) {
            e.submitParams.duration = timeTotal - timeLeft;
        });
        $('#exr-submit').on('click', function (e) {
            if(window.confirm('确定要提交试卷吗?')){
                $('.item.active > .exercise-view', '#exercise-list').trigger('next.hsk.test');
                $('#exercise-list').exerciseTest('submit', true).done(function (data) {
                    window.location.href = '/vi/5/4/report?pid=' + data.exam_id;
                });
            }
        });
        function activeAnswerSheetPanel(index) {
            var $collapse = $('li[data-slide-to=' + index + ']', '#answer-sheets').closest('.collapse');
            if (!$collapse.hasClass('in')) {
                $collapse.prev('.panel-heading').find('[data-toggle=collapse]').trigger('click');
            }
        }
        activeAnswerSheetPanel(0);
        window.setTimeout(function () {
            $('.item.active', '#exercise-list').data('autoPlayed', 1).find('.circle-audio').autoPlay();
        }, 1000);

jQuery('#emw-34fcb4d5').on('show.bs.modal', function(event){
    if(event.relatedTarget){
        var el = $(event.relatedTarget), url = el.attr('href') || el.data('url'), frm = $('iframe', this), 
        self = $(this), e = $.Event('beforeLoading.wm', {relatedTarget: el, url: url, loadingUrl : url});
        self.trigger(e);
        if(frm.data('_url') !== e.url){
            var title = el.data('title') || el.attr('title');
            title && $('.modal-title', this).html(title);
            frm.attr('src', e.loadingUrl).data('_url', e.url).parent().addClass('loading');
            self.trigger('afterLoading.wm', e.loadingUrl);
        }
    }
}).find('iframe').on('load', function() {
    $(this).height($(this.contentDocument).height()).parent().removeClass('loading');
});
